	reestablish_the_state_of_idaho = {
		##Reform a State from Nevada's territory
		cost = 100
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			AND = {
                original_tag = ERB
            }
		}
		visible = { 
			AND = {
				NOT = { 
					country_exists = HIG
				} 
				ERB = {
					OR = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 18
						has_full_control_of_state = 30
						has_full_control_of_state = 52
						has_full_control_of_state = 116
						has_full_control_of_state = 140
						has_full_control_of_state = 172
						has_full_control_of_state = 198
						has_full_control_of_state = 278
						has_full_control_of_state = 280
						has_full_control_of_state = 281
						has_full_control_of_state = 290
						has_full_control_of_state = 365
						has_full_control_of_state = 379
						has_full_control_of_state = 400
						has_full_control_of_state = 435
						has_full_control_of_state = 578
						has_full_control_of_state = 590
						has_full_control_of_state = 595
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				ERB = {
					has_completed_focus = enc_pacific_commonwealth
					OR = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 18
						has_full_control_of_state = 30
						has_full_control_of_state = 52
						has_full_control_of_state = 116
						has_full_control_of_state = 140
						has_full_control_of_state = 172
						has_full_control_of_state = 198
						has_full_control_of_state = 278
						has_full_control_of_state = 280
						has_full_control_of_state = 281
						has_full_control_of_state = 290
						has_full_control_of_state = 365
						has_full_control_of_state = 379
						has_full_control_of_state = 400
						has_full_control_of_state = 435
						has_full_control_of_state = 578
						has_full_control_of_state = 590
						has_full_control_of_state = 595
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = idaho_reestablish_text
			hidden_effect = {
				##Corring
				HIG = { 
					add_state_core = 18
					add_state_core = 30
					add_state_core = 52
					add_state_core = 116
					add_state_core = 140
					add_state_core = 172
					add_state_core = 198
					add_state_core = 278
					add_state_core = 280
					add_state_core = 281
					add_state_core = 290
					add_state_core = 365
					add_state_core = 379
					add_state_core = 400
					add_state_core = 435
					add_state_core = 578
					add_state_core = 590
					add_state_core = 595
				}

				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = HIG
					}
					HIG = {
						transfer_state = THIS
					}
				}

				any_allied_country = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = HIG
						}
						HIG = {
							transfer_state = THIS
						}
					}
				}

				##Capital
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 18 }} HIG = { set_capital = 18 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 30 }} HIG = { set_capital = 30 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 52 }} HIG = { set_capital = 52 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 116 }} HIG = { set_capital = 116 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 140 }} HIG = { set_capital = 140 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 172 }} HIG = { set_capital = 172 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 198 }} HIG = { set_capital = 198 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 278 }} HIG = { set_capital = 278 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 280 }} HIG = { set_capital = 280 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 281 }} HIG = { set_capital = 281 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 290 }} HIG = { set_capital = 290 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 365 }} HIG = { set_capital = 365 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 379 }} HIG = { set_capital = 379 }}

				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 590 }} HIG = { set_capital = 590 }}
				if = { limit = { HIG = { has_full_control_of_state = 595 }} HIG = { set_capital = 595 }}
				##Politics
				HIG = {
					set_stability = 0.45
					set_war_support = 0.30
					set_popularities = {
						people = 15
						elites = 10

					set_politics = {

					}
					create_country_leader  = {

					}
					add_ideas = disarmed_nation

					add_ideas = undesirables_law_none
					add_ideas = officer_law_local_heroes
					add_ideas = training_law_wasteland
					add_ideas = scavenging_law
					add_ideas = limited_exports
					add_ideas = currencygenericcap
					add_ideas = political_effort_censorship
					add_ideas = slavery_outlawed
					add_ideas = chems_banned
					load_focus_tree = owbhinasters_nevada_puppet
				##Tech
					set_research_slots = 3

							air_tech_level_tribal = 1
							#air_tech_level_settler = 1`
							naval_tech_level_tribal = 1
							naval_tech_level_settler = 1
							tools_tech_level_tribal = 1
							#tools_tech_level_settler = 1
							#tools_tech_level_scientific = 1
							habitation_tech_level_tribal = 1

                original_tag = ERB

					}

				}

						is_core_of = HIH
					}

						transfer_state = THIS
					}
				}

				any_allied_country = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = HIH
						}

							transfer_state = THIS
						}
					}
				}

				##Capital

##Louisiana
	reestablish_the_state_of_louisiana = {
		##Reform a State from Nevada's territory
		cost = 100
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			AND = {
                original_tag = ERB
            }
		}
		visible = { 
			AND = {
				NOT = { 
					country_exists = HIP 
				} 
				ERB = {
					OR = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 870
						has_full_control_of_state = 871
						has_full_control_of_state = 872
						has_full_control_of_state = 873
						has_full_control_of_state = 874
						has_full_control_of_state = 875
						has_full_control_of_state = 876
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				ERB = {
					has_completed_focus = enc_home_is_nevada
					OR = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 870
						has_full_control_of_state = 871
						has_full_control_of_state = 872
						has_full_control_of_state = 873
						has_full_control_of_state = 874
						has_full_control_of_state = 875
						has_full_control_of_state = 876
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = louisiana_reestablish_text
			hidden_effect = {
				##Corring
				HIP = { 
					add_state_core = 870
					add_state_core = 871 
					add_state_core = 872 
					add_state_core = 873 
					add_state_core = 874 
					add_state_core = 875 
					add_state_core = 876 
				}

				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = HIP
					}
					HIP = {
						transfer_state = THIS
					}
				}

				any_allied_country = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = HIP
						}
						HIP = {
							transfer_state = THIS
						}
					}
				}

				##Capital
				if = { limit = { HIP = { has_full_control_of_state = 870 }} HIP = { set_capital = 870 }}
				if = { limit = { HIP = { has_full_control_of_state = 871 }} HIP = { set_capital = 871 }}
				if = { limit = { HIP = { has_full_control_of_state = 872 }} HIP = { set_capital = 872 }}
				if = { limit = { HIP = { has_full_control_of_state = 873 }} HIP = { set_capital = 873 }}
				if = { limit = { HIP = { has_full_control_of_state = 874 }} HIP = { set_capital = 874 }}
				if = { limit = { HIP = { has_full_control_of_state = 875 }} HIP = { set_capital = 875 }}
				if = { limit = { HIP = { has_full_control_of_state = 876 }} HIP = { set_capital = 876 }}
				##Politics
				HIP = {
					set_stability = 0.45
					set_war_support = 0.30
					set_popularities = {
						people = 15
						elites = 10
						intellectuals = 70
						ruler = 5
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = intellectuals
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					create_country_leader  = {
						name = "Louisiana Provisional Government"
						desc = "HIP_DESC"
						picture = "portrait_Louisiana_PG.dds" ##gfx/leaders/HIP/

						traits = {}
					}
					add_ideas = disarmed_nation
					add_ideas = outsider_law_volunteers
					add_ideas = undesirables_law_none
					add_ideas = officer_law_local_heroes
					add_ideas = training_law_wasteland
					add_ideas = scavenging_law
					add_ideas = limited_exports
					add_ideas = currencygenericcap
					add_ideas = political_effort_censorship
					add_ideas = slavery_outlawed
					add_ideas = chems_banned
					load_focus_tree = owbhinasters_nevada_puppet
				##Tech
					set_research_slots = 3
					set_technology = {
						##Tech Levels
							infantry_tech_level_tribal = 1
							infantry_tech_level_settler = 1
							infantry_tech_level_scientific = 0

							air_tech_level_tribal = 1
							#air_tech_level_settler = 1`
							naval_tech_level_tribal = 1
							naval_tech_level_settler = 1
							tools_tech_level_tribal = 1
							#tools_tech_level_settler = 1
							#tools_tech_level_scientific = 1
							habitation_tech_level_tribal = 1
							#habitation_tech_level_settler = 1
							exploitation_tech_level_tribal = 1
							#exploitation_tech_level_settler = 1
							electronics_tech_level_tribal = 1
							#electronics_tech_level_settler = 1
						##Infantry Tech
							standard_weaponry_tech = 1
